Hotel with super convenient transportation and great service!
beginning:
Sichuan has been extremely hot at 44 degrees these days, so I came to Dalian to escape the summer and blow the sea breeze. Because it is a vacation, it is very convenient to take the subway directly from the airport to the downstairs of the hotel. The hotel is very new, and it is also very close to Venice Street across the street. Anyway, it is highly recommended!
hotel service:
The best thing about Fraser Court is that the room comes with its own kitchen and washing machine. Everything is ready to make a simple meal. Of course, if you stir fry, I suggest that you forget it, and it is completely okay to cook something simple. The front desk staff at the swimming pool (the lady) was very kind and helped me to solve the problem of forgetting my password in embarrassment, and also because we came from the south without a swimming cap. (In other words, I have never seen anyone wearing a swimming cap in the South Pool).
Surrounding:
The hotel is on the Kaidan Plaza, and the 4th floor is directly linked to the Kaidan food floor, which is so happy. If you make your own food, there is a supermarket downstairs on the first floor and it is convenient to buy clothes.
travel:
Venice is very close, you can walk there. It is very convenient to take a taxi from other places within 20!
Summarize:
The hotel is great! I will recognize this place when I come here! Hahaha, the photos attached are from the vicinity of the hotel. The view and the pool ha!
